      • addCouponType

        public void addCouponType(TField param)
        Appends the specified CouponType to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: If the bank wishes to use the Corporate Actions system to process their coupons this field will contain the ID ofthe DIARY.TYPE that they will use to process coupon payments. If this field is entered then the system will cyclethe INT.PAYMENT.DATE field on the SECURITY.MASTER record for the security concerned when a coupon is processed forthe security. Also if this field has been updated then DIARY records will automatically be created by DIV.AUT.REQand EOD.DIV.AUT.REQ instead of DIV.COUP.CUS records. Validation Rules: Must exist on the DIARY.TYPE file. Optional Input. If a DIARY.TYPE ID is entered here then the DIARY.TYPE record must be a CASH only record.

        Parameters:
        param - the CouponType to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addDefaultSuffix

        public void addDefaultSuffix(java.lang.CharSequence param)
        Appends the specified DefaultSuffix to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines whether, and for which modules, the Security valuation process will automatically assign deals for acustomer which have not been specifically assigned to a portfolio to a default portfolio. This field will be used by valuations update module to determine the customers portfolio when receivingnon-securities data. If a portfolio is not entered on the transaction then the system will assign a defaultdepending on the application supplying the data and this being in this field and also ensuring the customer is alsoa Securities customer. Example If customer number 123456 has two portfolios, 123456-1 and 123456-2, and they do a FOREX trade in whichthe PORTFOLIO.NUMBER field is left blank then a If this field is left blank then the deal will not be included on any portfolio valuation for this customer. b If FX or ALL is entered in this field then T24 will default to the first portfolio it finds for this customer(123456-1) that has not been closed and include the deal on that valuation. If all portfolios for this customer areclosed then the first portfolio will be assigned. Validation Rules: 0 to 3 Alphabetic characters (Multi-value field) (Optional input) Only the following values are allowed: Null - No applications will default. ALL - All applications will default.MM, FX etc which will be validated against the APPLICATIONS field in the COMPANY record

        Parameters:
        param - the DefaultSuffix to append
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void clearCouponType()

        Field description: If the bank wishes to use the Corporate Actions system to process their coupons this field will contain the ID ofthe DIARY.TYPE that they will use to process coupon payments. If this field is entered then the system will cyclethe INT.PAYMENT.DATE field on the SECURITY.MASTER record for the security concerned when a coupon is processed forthe security. Also if this field has been updated then DIARY records will automatically be created by DIV.AUT.REQand EOD.DIV.AUT.REQ instead of DIV.COUP.CUS records. Validation Rules: Must exist on the DIARY.TYPE file. Optional Input. If a DIARY.TYPE ID is entered here then the DIARY.TYPE record must be a CASH only record.

      • clearDefaultSuffix

        public void clearDefaultSuffix()
        Clear the collection of DefaultSuffix
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines whether, and for which modules, the Security valuation process will automatically assign deals for acustomer which have not been specifically assigned to a portfolio to a default portfolio. This field will be used by valuations update module to determine the customers portfolio when receivingnon-securities data. If a portfolio is not entered on the transaction then the system will assign a defaultdepending on the application supplying the data and this being in this field and also ensuring the customer is alsoa Securities customer. Example If customer number 123456 has two portfolios, 123456-1 and 123456-2, and they do a FOREX trade in whichthe PORTFOLIO.NUMBER field is left blank then a If this field is left blank then the deal will not be included on any portfolio valuation for this customer. b If FX or ALL is entered in this field then T24 will default to the first portfolio it finds for this customer(123456-1) that has not been closed and include the deal on that valuation. If all portfolios for this customer areclosed then the first portfolio will be assigned. Validation Rules: 0 to 3 Alphabetic characters (Multi-value field) (Optional input) Only the following values are allowed: Null - No applications will default. ALL - All applications will default.MM, FX etc which will be validated against the APPLICATIONS field in the COMPANY record

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        nothing

        Returns the CaFeeAdjust

        Field description: For cash corporate actions, the fees should be adjusted so that it does not exceed the cash amount. If the field is set as NET, the fee will be adjusted to the extent of net amount of dividend due. If the field is set as GROSS, the fee will be adjusted to the extent of the dividend amount. This will resultin a debit to the client account if there are source or local taxes and other charges For eg:- Dividend amount is USD100. Taxes or charges on dividend is USD12. Calculated Fees is 110. If this field is NET, then fee will be adjusted to USD 88. If this field is GROSS, fee will be adjusted toUSD100 and there will be a net debit of USD12 to the customer. Validation Rules Allowed value are GROSS , NET

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CaFeeAdjust

        Returns the collection of DefaultSuffix

        Field description: Defines whether, and for which modules, the Security valuation process will automatically assign deals for acustomer which have not been specifically assigned to a portfolio to a default portfolio. This field will be used by valuations update module to determine the customers portfolio when receivingnon-securities data. If a portfolio is not entered on the transaction then the system will assign a defaultdepending on the application supplying the data and this being in this field and also ensuring the customer is alsoa Securities customer. Example If customer number 123456 has two portfolios, 123456-1 and 123456-2, and they do a FOREX trade in whichthe PORTFOLIO.NUMBER field is left blank then a If this field is left blank then the deal will not be included on any portfolio valuation for this customer. b If FX or ALL is entered in this field then T24 will default to the first portfolio it finds for this customer(123456-1) that has not been closed and include the deal on that valuation. If all portfolios for this customer areclosed then the first portfolio will be assigned. Validation Rules: 0 to 3 Alphabetic characters (Multi-value field) (Optional input) Only the following values are allowed: Null - No applications will default. ALL - All applications will default.MM, FX etc which will be validated against the APPLICATIONS field in the COMPANY record

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        List<TField> -

        Field description: This field defines the method to use when calculating the margin value. This may be by asset only or by bothasset and liability. Where BOTH is entered, the asset value will be calculated as stated above and the liability value will becalculated using the LOSS.MARGIN.RATE from ASSET.TYPE, SUB.ASSET.TYPE or ASSET.BY.CATEG Where this field is left blank, both asset and liability values will be calculated based on the MARGIN.RATEfield.       • getNavType

        public TField getNavType()
        Returns the NavType

        Field description: This field allows the NAV to be recorded either NET or GROSS of transaction costs. When processing SEC.TRADE and SECURITY.TRANSFER records,it is possible to record the NAV either Net or Gross oftransaction costs. If NET is selected then,the cost of the acquisition is NAV plus all charges and commissions, and the sale consideration is NAV minus charges and commissions. If GROSS is selected then charges and commissions are ignored. The difference between the cost of acquisition and sale consideration is considered as the Capital gain andtaxed accordingly.

      • getOverTradeUnit

        public TField getOverTradeUnit()
        Returns the OverTradeUnit

        Field description: YES/NO flag to allow the bank to specify whether they want to allow transactions to be entered where the nominalof the securities on the customer side is not exactly divisible by the number of trading units or not. If thisfield is set to YES then if a Securities transaction is entered where the number of nominal on the customer side isnot exactly divisible by the number of trading units for the Security concerned an override will result. The brokerside will never allow the input of a nominal figure that is not exactly divisible by the number of trading units ofthe Security. If the field is set to NO all nominals entered must be exactly divisible by the number of TradingUnits defined on the SECURITY.MASTER record for the Security Concerned. Validation Rules: Input restricted to YES or NO.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The OverTradeUnit

      • getParValueInt

        public TField getParValueInt()
        Returns the ParValueInt

        Field description: This field controls whether the value of the PAR.VALUE of a security (as set-up in the PAR.VALUE field onSECURITY.MASTER) is used in the calculation of the interest amount for bonds or not. If this field is set to YES then the par value of a bond will be included in any interest amount calculation.For example, if a bond has a par value of 2.00 dollars, an interest day basis of 360/360, an interest rate of 10 %,and two equal payments a year then the interest amount for a portfolio holding 100,000 bonds for a half year (180days) payment is AMOUNT = (180 * 10.00 * 100,000 * 2) --------------------------- (360 * 100) If this field is set to NO then the value of the PAR.VALUE field is ignored and for the example given above theinterest amount will be calculated AMOUNT = (180 * 10.00 * 100,000) ----------------------- (360 * 100) Validation Rules: Only input of YES or NO allowed. Will default to NO.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The ParValueInt

        public void insertCouponType(TField param, int pos)
        Insert the specified CouponType to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: If the bank wishes to use the Corporate Actions system to process their coupons this field will contain the ID ofthe DIARY.TYPE that they will use to process coupon payments. If this field is entered then the system will cyclethe INT.PAYMENT.DATE field on the SECURITY.MASTER record for the security concerned when a coupon is processed forthe security. Also if this field has been updated then DIARY records will automatically be created by DIV.AUT.REQand EOD.DIV.AUT.REQ instead of DIV.COUP.CUS records. Validation Rules: Must exist on the DIARY.TYPE file. Optional Input. If a DIARY.TYPE ID is entered here then the DIARY.TYPE record must be a CASH only record.

        Parameters:
        param - the CouponType to append
        pos - The position where to insert the value.

      • insertDefaultSuffix

        public void insertDefaultSuffix(java.lang.CharSequence param, int pos)
        Insert the specified DefaultSuffix to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines whether, and for which modules, the Security valuation process will automatically assign deals for acustomer which have not been specifically assigned to a portfolio to a default portfolio. This field will be used by valuations update module to determine the customers portfolio when receivingnon-securities data. If a portfolio is not entered on the transaction then the system will assign a defaultdepending on the application supplying the data and this being in this field and also ensuring the customer is alsoa Securities customer. Example If customer number 123456 has two portfolios, 123456-1 and 123456-2, and they do a FOREX trade in whichthe PORTFOLIO.NUMBER field is left blank then a If this field is left blank then the deal will not be included on any portfolio valuation for this customer. b If FX or ALL is entered in this field then T24 will default to the first portfolio it finds for this customer(123456-1) that has not been closed and include the deal on that valuation. If all portfolios for this customer areclosed then the first portfolio will be assigned. Validation Rules: 0 to 3 Alphabetic characters (Multi-value field) (Optional input) Only the following values are allowed: Null - No applications will default. ALL - All applications will default.MM, FX etc which will be validated against the APPLICATIONS field in the COMPANY record

        Parameters:
        param - the DefaultSuffix to append
        pos - The position where to insert the value.
        Returns:
        nothing

      • removeCouponType

        public void removeCouponType(int idx)
        Remove the CouponType at the specified position in this collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: If the bank wishes to use the Corporate Actions system to process their coupons this field will contain the ID ofthe DIARY.TYPE that they will use to process coupon payments. If this field is entered then the system will cyclethe INT.PAYMENT.DATE field on the SECURITY.MASTER record for the security concerned when a coupon is processed forthe security. Also if this field has been updated then DIARY records will automatically be created by DIV.AUT.REQand EOD.DIV.AUT.REQ instead of DIV.COUP.CUS records. Validation Rules: Must exist on the DIARY.TYPE file. Optional Input. If a DIARY.TYPE ID is entered here then the DIARY.TYPE record must be a CASH only record.

      • removeDefaultSuffix

        public void removeDefaultSuffix(int idx)
        Remove the DefaultSuffix at the specified position in this collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines whether, and for which modules, the Security valuation process will automatically assign deals for acustomer which have not been specifically assigned to a portfolio to a default portfolio. This field will be used by valuations update module to determine the customers portfolio when receivingnon-securities data. If a portfolio is not entered on the transaction then the system will assign a defaultdepending on the application supplying the data and this being in this field and also ensuring the customer is alsoa Securities customer. Example If customer number 123456 has two portfolios, 123456-1 and 123456-2, and they do a FOREX trade in whichthe PORTFOLIO.NUMBER field is left blank then a If this field is left blank then the deal will not be included on any portfolio valuation for this customer. b If FX or ALL is entered in this field then T24 will default to the first portfolio it finds for this customer(123456-1) that has not been closed and include the deal on that valuation. If all portfolios for this customer areclosed then the first portfolio will be assigned. Validation Rules: 0 to 3 Alphabetic characters (Multi-value field) (Optional input) Only the following values are allowed: Null - No applications will default. ALL - All applications will default.MM, FX etc which will be validated against the APPLICATIONS field in the COMPANY record

        Parameters:
        idx - index of the element to remove
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCaFeeAdjust

        public void setCaFeeAdjust(TField value)
        Set the specified value for CaFeeAdjust
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: For cash corporate actions, the fees should be adjusted so that it does not exceed the cash amount. If the field is set as NET, the fee will be adjusted to the extent of net amount of dividend due. If the field is set as GROSS, the fee will be adjusted to the extent of the dividend amount. This will resultin a debit to the client account if there are source or local taxes and other charges For eg:- Dividend amount is USD100. Taxes or charges on dividend is USD12. Calculated Fees is 110. If this field is NET, then fee will be adjusted to USD 88. If this field is GROSS, fee will be adjusted toUSD100 and there will be a net debit of USD12 to the customer. Validation Rules Allowed value are GROSS , NET

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setCalcClosedport(TField value)
        Set the specified value for CalcClosedport
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Field to provide an option to switch off the calculations on closed customer portfolios in order to increase the performance of some of the securities related COB jobs listed below. EOD.PERFORM.UPDATE, SC.EOM.UPDATE and WRITE.SC.VAL.EXTRACT A portfolio will only be considered as closed if the following conditions apply, 1)Closure date in SEC.ACC.MASTER is less than the current system/bank date 2)If safekeeping fees are setup then the fees must be posted or zero in SAFEKEEP.HOLDING 3)If advisory fees are setup then the fees must be posted or zero in SC.ADVISORY.CHG This parameter will only apply to customer portfolios, dealer books will not be ignored. If this field is set to NO, any calculation on closed portfolios will be switched off.

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

MULTIPLE - Each restriction test that fails will be displayed to the user in turn, therefore if 20 tests failthe user will see 20 error messages. NO.CONS.CHECK - No Security Constraints check will happen as system will skip Constraint check processing in Security transactions. Validation Rules: SINGLE, MULTIPLE,NO.CONS.CHECK or NULL. (If NULL the systems assumes SINGLE mode)

      • setDefaultSuffix

        public void setDefaultSuffix(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)
        Set the specified DefaultSuffix to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines whether, and for which modules, the Security valuation process will automatically assign deals for acustomer which have not been specifically assigned to a portfolio to a default portfolio. This field will be used by valuations update module to determine the customers portfolio when receivingnon-securities data. If a portfolio is not entered on the transaction then the system will assign a defaultdepending on the application supplying the data and this being in this field and also ensuring the customer is alsoa Securities customer. Example If customer number 123456 has two portfolios, 123456-1 and 123456-2, and they do a FOREX trade in whichthe PORTFOLIO.NUMBER field is left blank then a If this field is left blank then the deal will not be included on any portfolio valuation for this customer. b If FX or ALL is entered in this field then T24 will default to the first portfolio it finds for this customer(123456-1) that has not been closed and include the deal on that valuation. If all portfolios for this customer areclosed then the first portfolio will be assigned. Validation Rules: 0 to 3 Alphabetic characters (Multi-value field) (Optional input) Only the following values are allowed: Null - No applications will default. ALL - All applications will default.MM, FX etc which will be validated against the APPLICATIONS field in the COMPANY record

        Parameters:
        param - the DefaultSuffix to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

If set to AUTH then the authorised value of the transaction will be included on the valuation. Note that changeswhere the customer is deleted or the portfolio changed are not included on the valuation for this setting. Validation Rules: Valid input YES, NO or AUTH. Default NO.

      • setMarginValue

        public void setMarginValue(TField value)
        Set the specified value for MarginValue
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field defines the method to use when calculating the margin value. This may be by asset only or by bothasset and liability. Where ASSET is entered, all asset margin values will be calculated using the respectiveMARGIN.RATE in either ASSET.TYPE, SUB.ASSET.TYPE or ASSET.BY.CATEG and liability values will be 0. Where BOTH is entered, the asset value will be calculated as stated above and the liability value will becalculated using the LOSS.MARGIN.RATE from ASSET.TYPE, SUB.ASSET.TYPE or ASSET.BY.CATEG Where this field is left blank, both asset and liability values will be calculated based on the MARGIN.RATEfield. Validation Rules: Input must be ASSET, BOTH or null

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setNavType

        public void setNavType(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for NavType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field allows the NAV to be recorded either NET or GROSS of transaction costs. When processing SEC.TRADE and SECURITY.TRANSFER records,it is possible to record the NAV either Net or Gross oftransaction costs. If NET is selected then,the cost of the acquisition is NAV plus all charges and commissions, and the sale consideration is NAV minus charges and commissions. If GROSS is selected then charges and commissions are ignored. The difference between the cost of acquisition and sale consideration is considered as the Capital gain andtaxed accordingly.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setOpnOrdFwdAcct(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for OpnOrdFwdAcct
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field controls whether or not forward accounting entries are generated by SEC.OPEN.ORDER. Allows NONE, NO, Y, UNAUTH, DEBIT and DEBIT.UNAUTH NO or NONE - This setting indicates no accounting entries will be generated at any stage of the process. UNAUTH - This setting allows STMT.ENTRY records to be generated at the unauthorised stage. Suitable ACCOUNTbalance messages and the appropriate OVERRIDE messages will be generated. DEBIT - This indicates only forward debit entries will be generated for the customer at authorised stage DEBIT.UNAUTH - This indicates forward debit entries will be generated for the customer at unauthorised stage itself. Y - This setting produces suitable ACCOUNT balance messages and the appropriate OVERRIDE messages will be storedon the transaction. However, STMT.ENTRY records will only be generated at authorization stage.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setOverTradeUnit

        public void setOverTradeUnit(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for OverTradeUnit
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: YES/NO flag to allow the bank to specify whether they want to allow transactions to be entered where the nominalof the securities on the customer side is not exactly divisible by the number of trading units or not. If thisfield is set to YES then if a Securities transaction is entered where the number of nominal on the customer side isnot exactly divisible by the number of trading units for the Security concerned an override will result. The brokerside will never allow the input of a nominal figure that is not exactly divisible by the number of trading units ofthe Security. If the field is set to NO all nominals entered must be exactly divisible by the number of TradingUnits defined on the SECURITY.MASTER record for the Security Concerned. Validation Rules: Input restricted to YES or NO.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setParValueInt

        public void setParValueInt(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for ParValueInt
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field controls whether the value of the PAR.VALUE of a security (as set-up in the PAR.VALUE field onSECURITY.MASTER) is used in the calculation of the interest amount for bonds or not. If this field is set to YES then the par value of a bond will be included in any interest amount calculation.For example, if a bond has a par value of 2.00 dollars, an interest day basis of 360/360, an interest rate of 10 %,and two equal payments a year then the interest amount for a portfolio holding 100,000 bonds for a half year (180days) payment is AMOUNT = (180 * 10.00 * 100,000 * 2) --------------------------- (360 * 100) If this field is set to NO then the value of the PAR.VALUE field is ignored and for the example given above theinterest amount will be calculated AMOUNT = (180 * 10.00 * 100,000) ----------------------- (360 * 100) Validation Rules: Only input of YES or NO allowed. Will default to NO.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used to specify whether the recoverable tax should be included in the valuation and performancecalculation. CUM The recoverable Tax will be accumulated and shown in valuation files (SC.POS.ASSET and SC.VALUATION.EXTRACT)as field REC.TAX.CUM.AMT. This field will be reset to 0 when the Reset occurs through the EOD processEOD.RECOVERABLE.TAX. This option is only available if AM is installed. BOOK - The recoverable tax amount will be added to the valuation tables on the same day and will not be accumulated. Validation Rules: field (A) field. Allowed values are CUM BOOK. If left Blank considered as BOOK.

        Field description: Defines whether the cost of position fields in the SECURITY.POSITION application will be maintained on a tradedate or a value date basis. UPFRONT.PAYMENT criteria follows below logic: If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is not YES or DIARY is NO, then event is not eligible for upfront payment If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is YES and SC.PARAMETER is NO and DIARY is blank, then event is not eligible for upfront payment All other cases apart from above are eligible for upfront payment.         Set the specified value for ValuationSubr
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies the company specific valuation sub-routine that will be used to produce the customer or internalvaluation reports as defined in the CUSTOMER.SECURITY, SEC.ACC.MASTER or OL.VAL.REPS applications. Since every bank is likely to have special requirements vis-a-vis the layout of its valuation reports, thisfield will allow the easy implementation of different reports at different T24 sites and even for differentcompanies on the same machine. If no value is entered is this field then the system will use the default valuation sub-routineSC.ASSET.VAL.REPORTS. If the company is entered (XXXX) this will default to SC.ASSET.VAL.REPORTS.XXXX. Validation Rules: 1 - 27 Alphanumeric characters. (Optional Input) Must exist as a Verb in the VOC.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setYieldType

        public void setYieldType(TField value)
        Set the specified value for YieldType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field controls whether the current yield or the yield to maturity is used in the update of Sc.Cash.Flow andSc.Pos.Asset. If this field is set to 1 then the yield to maturity will be used from the Security.Supp record. If this field is set to 2 then the current yield will be used from the Security.Supp record. See the helptext for Sc.Pos.Asset, yield, for a more detailed explanation Validation Rules: Only input of 1 or 2 allowed. Will default to 1.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing
